country_event = {
    id = 18490001
    title = "The Conquest of Odiene"
    desc = "ODIENEKABADUGU"
    picture = "kabadugu_map"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = KNG
		owns = 3769
		1896 = { empty = yes }
		year = 1848
		month = 5
		DJK = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "We should flee, and fast!"
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					1896 = { empty = yes }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				1896 = {
					secede_province = THIS life_rating = 25 any_pop = { literacy = -0.99 }
				}
			}
		}
		3881 = { any_pop = { limit = { type = soldiers } reduce_pop = 3 } }
		DJK = {
			all_core = { remove_core = DJK }
			primary_culture = dyula
			add_accepted_culture = senufo
			add_accepted_culture = western_nigritic
			remove_accepted_culture = kurdish
			government = absolute_monarchy
                    activate_technology = flintlock_rifles
                    set_country_flag = using_foreign_weapons
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					owns = 3769
				}
			}
			owner = {
				3769 = {
					secede_province = DJK
					add_core = DJK
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					owns = 3881
				}
			}
			owner = {
				3881 = {
					secede_province = DJK
					add_core = DJK
				}
			}
		}
		DJK = { government = absolute_monarchy }
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		693 = { secede_province = THIS secede_province = DJK }

		693 = {
			# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
			secede_province = THIS
			# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
			secede_province = NULL
		}
    }
    option = {

			limit = {
				owner = {
					1896 = { empty = yes }
				}
			}

				}
			}
		}
		3881 = { any_pop = { limit = { type = soldiers } reduce_pop = 3 } }
		DJK = {
			all_core = { remove_core = DJK }
			primary_culture = dyula
			add_accepted_culture = senufo
			add_accepted_culture = western_nigritic
			remove_accepted_culture = kurdish
                    activate_technology = flintlock_rifles
                    set_country_flag = using_foreign_weapons
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {

					owns = 3769

			}

				3769 = {

country_event = {
    id = 184900011
    title = "The Gwiriko Rebellion"
    desc = "Gwiriko has started a revolt against our rule, as its Dyula population demands less discrimination and more control over the taxing of the region."
    picture = "kabadugu_map"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = KNG
		owns = 1898
		year = 1856
		month = 5
		NOT = { year = 1858 }
		BDN = { exists = no }
		GUK = { exists = no }
		has_global_flag = wargwirikohappened
		NOT = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "To war!"
		any_owned = { limit = { OR = {
				province_id = 1905
				province_id = 1906
				province_id = 3764
				province_id = 1898
			} }
			secede_province = BDN
			add_core = BDN
		}
		war = {
			target = BDN
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = conquest_any }
			defender_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
		}
    }
    option = {
        name = "For Gwiriko! §BPlay as Gwiriko§W"
		any_owned = { limit = { OR = {
				province_id = 1905
				province_id = 1906
				province_id = 3764
				province_id = 1898
			} }
			secede_province = BDN
			add_core = BDN
		}
		war = {
			target = BDN
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = conquest_any }
			defender_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
		}
		change_tag_no_core_switch = BDN
    }

}
country_event = {
    id = 18490002
    title = "The Kong-Gwiriko War of $YEAR$"
    desc = "GWIRIKOCHANGE"
    picture = "kong_map"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = GUK
		neighbour = BDN
		BDN = { exists = no }
		KNG = { is_vassal = no exists = yes }
		year = 1850
		month = 2
		NOT = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "For Gwiriko!"
		set_global_flag = wargwirikohappened
		BDN = {
			all_core = { remove_core = BDN }
			capital = 1082
			primary_culture = gur
			add_accepted_culture = bambara
			remove_accepted_culture = kurdish
			religion = fetishist
clr_country_flag = sunni_country
			set_country_flag = animist_country
                    activate_technology = flintlock_rifles
                    set_country_flag = using_foreign_weapons
		}
		change_tag = BDN
		government = absolute_monarchy
		GUK = { all_core = { remove_core = GUK } primary_culture = ukrainian add_accepted_culture = siberian remove_accepted_culture = gur remove_accepted_culture = bambara }
		war = {
			target = KNG
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
			defender_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
			call_ally = no
		}
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		693 = { secede_province = THIS secede_province = BDN }
		# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
		693 = {
			# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT
			secede_province = THIS
			# Audax Validator "." Ignore_NEXT

		}
    }

		tag = GMJ

            capital_scope = { continent = africa }

            capital_scope = { continent = east_africa }
            capital_scope = { continent = south_africa }

		government = theocracy
            GMJ = {
				all_core = { remove_core = GMJ }
				political_reform = no_slavery
				government = presidential_dictatorship
				primary_culture = han_chinese
				remove_accepted_culture = yoruba
				remove_accepted_culture = nupoid

				remove_accepted_culture = fulbe

					ideology = socialist
					value = 0.4
				}

country_event = {

    id = 31716
    title = "EVTNAME31716" #Eiffel Tower Construction
    desc = "EVTDESC31716"
    picture = "eiffel_tower_construction"

	fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = "EVT31716OPTA"
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 40000 }
                    NOT = { check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 1 } }
                }
            }
            owner = { set_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 40 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 40000 }
                    check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 9 }
                }
            }
            owner = { change_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 40 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { money = 40000 } }
            owner = { treasury = -40000 }
        }
        random_list = {

country_event = {
    id = 18482475
    title = "The Senussi Movement is Founded"
    desc = "SENUSSICREATION"

    fire_only_once = yes

		owns = 1736
		year = 1843
		CYR = { exists = no }
    }

    option = {
        name = "Oh no..."
		CYR = {
			government = absolute_monarchy all_core = { remove_core = CYR }
			capital = 1735
			primary_culture = maghrebi
			add_accepted_culture = bedouin
			add_accepted_culture = teda
			add_accepted_culture = berber
			add_accepted_culture = tuareg
			military_reform = yes_foreign_weapons
			remove_accepted_culture = nupoid
			remove_accepted_culture = yoruba
			remove_accepted_culture = hausa
			remove_accepted_culture = east_kwa
		}
		1735 = { add_core = CYR }
		1736 = { add_core = CYR }
		1737 = { add_core = CYR }
		1738 = { add_core = CYR }
		1742 = { add_core = CYR }
		1754 = { add_core = CYR }
		1758 = { add_core = CYR }
		1817 = { add_core = CYR }

		}
